  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_966f45de-6e74-4d35-8817-6204c40aae19'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initAppleId();

      initializeSiwa();

  <span id="freeText8794751552381693238" style="display:none">From the NEW YORK TIMES bestselling author of WAIT FOR YOU, this is the story of Cam and Avery’s sizzling romance as you’ve never seen it before, told exclusively from Cam’s perspective…<br /><br />Cameron Hamilton is used to getting what he wants, especially when it comes to women. But when Avery Morgansten comes crashing into his life – literally – he finally meets the one person who can resist his soulful baby blues. But Cam’s not ready to give up – he can’t get this feisty and intriguing girl out of his head.<br /><br />Avery has secrets, secrets that keep her from admitting the feelings Cam knows she has for him. What will it take to help him break down her barriers and gain her trust? Or will he be shut out of Avery’s life, losing his first real shot at the kind of love that lasts forever?</span>

<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">I love it too! And yeah, go try books by Colleen Hoover (they're ALL amazing!) the Ten Tiny Breaths series by K.A. Tucker (I've reread this so many ti<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">I love it too! And yeah, go try books by Colleen Hoover (they're ALL amazing!) the Ten Tiny Breaths series by K.A. Tucker (I've reread this so many times!) and Abbi Glines (her Rosemary and Seabreeze series are my faves!) Beautiful Disaster has already been recommended but I'm adding it again because it is one of my all-time faves and it's the beginning of a series (all of which are amazing!) These are my fave authors (if you didn't notice... :) Enjoy!<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>

<div id="review_637016523" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/637016523" />
    <a title="Laura" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8429172-laura"><img alt="Laura" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1595453256p2/8429172.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/637016523?book_show_action=true">Jun 09, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Laura" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Laura" href="/user/show/8429172-laura">Laura</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=jlarmentrout-books">jlarmentrout-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=reading-slowly">reading-slowly</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=amazing-heroines">amazing-heroines</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=oh-my-panties">oh-my-panties</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=until-the-end-of-the-world">until-the-end-of-the-world</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=na">na</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=book-boyfriends">book-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=so-happy-i-read-this">so-happy-i-read-this</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer637016523" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14152355006437507281">So, this book really aged nicely. It's one of the few NA contemporary novels I read over and over whenever I feel the need and boy, it was as good as the first time. It still gives me the feels and has me giggling like a toddler. I wish all the romance books I read were like this one and the Off Campus series. <br/>__________________________<br/><br/><br/><br/>￼<br/><br/>|4,6 stars|<br/><br/><br/>Everything was okay. Maybe not perfect, but life wasn't meant to be perfect. It was messy and sometimes it was a disaster, but there was beauty in the</span>
  <span id="freeText14152355006437507281" style="display:none">So, this book really aged nicely. It's one of the few NA contemporary novels I read over and over whenever I feel the need and boy, it was as good as the first time. It still gives me the feels and has me giggling like a toddler. I wish all the romance books I read were like this one and the Off Campus series. <br />__________________________<br /><br /><br /><br />￼<br /><br />|4,6 stars|<br /><br /><br />Everything was okay. Maybe not perfect, but life wasn't meant to be perfect. It was messy and sometimes it was a disaster, but there was beauty in the messiness and there could be peace in the disaster.<br /><br />|Wait For You|<br /><br />Blurb: Cameron Hamilton is used to getting what he wants, especially when it comes to women. But when Avery Morgansten comes crashing into his life – literally – he finally meets the one person who can resist his soulful baby blues. But Cam’s not ready to give up – he can’t get this feisty and intriguing girl out of his head.<br />Avery has secrets, secrets that keep her from admitting the feelings Cam knows she has for him. What will it take to help him break down her barriers and gain her trust? Or will he be shut out of Avery’s life, losing his first real shot at the kind of love that lasts forever?<br /><br />￼<br /><br />Note #1: I’ve read this books several times since it came out but I hadn’t reviewed because I’m way too lazy but the time has come *sigh* and what an amazing time indeed.<br /><br />Note #2: This book’s a retelling of Wait for You from Cam’s POV and since I haven’t reviewed WFY because lazy af, you’ll find what the whole thing is about here.<br /><br />￼<br /><br />Alright, so both WFY and TIN tell the story of Avery and Cameron and how they get to leave their pasts behind in hopes to find a future together. Things can and should be easy but as secrets are revealed everything gets harder and harder.<br /><br />I adore this book and that’s not a secret and what’s not a secret either is the fact that I love this book more than WFY but, even though this one doesn’t really add much to the original story, I think it complements it really well. If I fell in love with Cam and Cam/Avery as a couple, I absolutely loved them all way more here and it also helps to understand lots of things.<br /><br />Ah, let’s start with our main lady.<br /><br />￼<br /><br />Avery’s a 19 years old girl who’s about to start college and she’s got issues. She used to dance and being popular but now all she wants is to survive and start over. She’s chosen a really far from home university in hopes to leave everything behind but her past comes to play and tries to screw with her present.<br /><br />Avery was raped 5 years ago when she was fourteen but her parents made her drop the charges and everyone turned on her. Her life was hell until she could go out of town, and while she’s not closed to friendship, she doesn’t trust people with her heart. She’s haunted by her past and though she tries to move on, the only thing she does is survive... until she bumps into Cam. <br /><br /><br />“You love me?”<br />I smiled slightly. “Yes, sweetheart.”<br />Avery held my gaze for a few moments, and I saw the very second she cracked. When the walls she had built around herself to just get by every day finally crumbled.<br /><br /><br /><br />￼<br /><br />I understand why some people couldn’t relate to Avery and while her and I didn’t have much in common aside from the fact that we both love Cam, history and dancing, she was still a very likeable character and I enjoyed her in WFY and TIN. <br /><br />Now, Cam.<br /><br />*sigh* How could I describe Cameron Hamilton?<br /><br />￼<br /><br />He’s one of my ultimate book boyfriends. He’s just so fucking swoon worthy.<br />Okay, so Cam’s all about having a good time. It can be with his friends, with his family, with his classmates or with girls but for a while now he’s been off. He’s not being partying that much lately and he isn’t feeling like his old self. <br /><br />He was supposed to be graduating this year but he had to take a year off and spent all those months doing community service and attending to some meetings to control his anger. Why? Because he beat the punk who was hitting his sister and the guy ended up in a coma. The kid woke up and Cam didn’t have it that bad but still. He can’t play soccer anymore and he’s afraid once he can, he’ll be too old for it so he’s happy working on sport therapy.<br /><br />The thing with Cam is that he’s so very dreamy. He’s kinda cocky but not too much and he’s charming as fucking fuck. He’s pretty sweet, sexy and quite nice. He’s basically the guy you introduce to your mother and the one who fucks your brain out later that night.<br /><br />￼<br /><br /><br />“Don’t worry. I know the truth.”<br />“The truth about what?”<br />“You want to say yes, but you’re just not ready.”<br />“It’s okay. I’m a lot to handle, but I can assure you, you’ll have fun handling me.”<br /><br /><br /><br />My love for Cam is out of this world but maybe that’s because he’s the ultimate dream, ya know? Like, what are the odds you bump into someone and that person turns out to be everything you’ve ever wanted and more? A sensitive guy who wants to marry the hell out of you and give you the best days and nights of your life? Cameron is absolutely perfect so he is the dream guy. He’s goals so maybe that’s why I love this book so much. It gives me hope.<br /><br />￼<br /><br /><br />I was glad she was asleep, because the thought of her knowing how badly my hands shook would probably have been embarrassing as hell. Boy, they were trembling too, like I'd never touched a girl before.<br />Avery...hell, she completely undid me.<br /><br /><br /><br />Is the book perfect? No, it isn’t. I want more backstory. I want to know how Cam was before and right after the incident with his sister’s ex. I want to read more about Avery early years and I want <br />all the books in this series to be only about Avery and Cam because they’re my favorite.<br />I’ve read the rest of the books so I know what’s going on but I can’t help myself.<br /><br />￼<br /><br />Anyhow, the dynamic between Avery and Cameron is quite different. He pushes but not too far because he knows something’s up with her and he really wants her to come around and while in most occasions I write off the guys who is hyper persistent over the girl, in Cameron’s case, I don’t. Maybe it was the fact that he charmed my pants out or maybe it was the fact that Avery wanted to be chased and charmed and loved so maybe that was it? We do need to realize when the chasing is good and when it turns out creepy.<br /><br /><br />“Shit,” I muttered, sitting back in the seat.<br />Avery ran again.<br />And I had the craziest urge to give chase.<br /><br /><br /><br />￼<br /><br />They truly work and they actually complement each other but without absorb each other. Does that make sense? Their relationship can only grow and grow and they can argue all they want but, in the end, they love each other too much to stay mad but they know when to walk away. The thing is, they adore each other but they still care about themselves. It’s not a toxic love where one would literally die without the other which it’s something it always bothers me in NA novels.<br /><br /><br />At first I didn’t know what to say. I . . . I had waited for Avery—I had waited for her for months. Hell, I would’ve waited for her for years, but she . . .<br />Turning my cheek, I pressed a kiss to the inside of her palm. “Thank you for trusting in me.”<br /><br /><br /><br />￼<br /><br />In conclusion, if you like swoon worthy sexy guys with big hearts and really funny times, you should definitely pick up Wait For You and then Trust In Me or read just one of them, it’s all good.<br /><br />￼</span>
  <a data-text-id="14152355006437507281" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/608299659?book_show_action=true">May 06, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer608299659" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15080761161676965726"><b>4.5 Cookie Stars!!!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/1ca1b57a-ad11-40f1-a3a6-a03ee2d40ac0_zps8961d33b.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382863626i/6246440.jpg' alt=' photo 1ca1b57a-ad11-40f1-a3a6-a03ee2d40ac0_zps8961d33b.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/>I’m just going to give a quick summary of <i>Trust in Me</i>... If you want the whole shebang, check out my full review of <i>Wait for You</i>: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/547676074'>https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a> , since this novella is the same story, just from Cam’s p.o.v.<br/><br/>Avery and Cam literally run in to each other on their first day of astronomy class. Cam is taken by this girl that reminds him of Strawberry Shortcake. He wants to know her. Avery is very standoffish. Something happened to her, something she is</span>
  <span id="freeText15080761161676965726" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Cookie Stars!!!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/1ca1b57a-ad11-40f1-a3a6-a03ee2d40ac0_zps8961d33b.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382863626i/6246440.jpg" alt=" photo 1ca1b57a-ad11-40f1-a3a6-a03ee2d40ac0_zps8961d33b.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>I’m just going to give a quick summary of <i>Trust in Me</i>... If you want the whole shebang, check out my full review of <i>Wait for You</i>: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/547676074">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a> , since this novella is the same story, just from Cam’s p.o.v.<br><br>Avery and Cam literally run in to each other on their first day of astronomy class. Cam is taken by this girl that reminds him of Strawberry Shortcake. He wants to know her. Avery is very standoffish. Something happened to her, something she isn’t ready to reveal to anyone. For the time being, Cam tries to be satisfied just being Avery’s friend, but it’s difficult. They both have strong feelings for one another. They both have pasts, secrets. Getting past them and being truthful with one another, trusting each other with the past is the only way they can ever really be with one another. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/e6751cd8-b424-437e-95b6-e8578fd66540_zps7c84f71a.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382960282i/6301893.jpg" alt=" photo e6751cd8-b424-437e-95b6-e8578fd66540_zps7c84f71a.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The very best part of this novella: Cam. The fact that it was in his pov, plus... I just love this guy! I mean, what isn’t to love??? He’s sweet, charming, funny and swoony. A perfect book boyfriend! Some of my favorite Cam quotes:<br><i>
  <blockquote>“I’m a shallow, shallow boy. Hey, it helps that you’re pretty. It brings out the nice guy in me. Makes me want to share my cookies with you.”<br> “So if I was ugly you wouldn’t be nice to me?”<br> “I’d still be nice to you if you were ugly.” <br>“Okay.”<br> “I just wouldn’t offer you my cookies.”<br><br>“You’re a good guy, Cam.” “No, I’m not. I’m only good with you.”<br><br>“Fuck, Avery. You think I don’t want you? There’s not a single part of you that I don’t want, you understand? I want to be on you and inside of you. I want you against the wall, on the couch, in your bed, in my bed, and every fucking place I can possibly think of, and trust me, I have a vast imagination when it comes to these kinds of things. Don’t ever doubt that I want you."<br><br>“Well, that was... really sort of perfect.”<br> “I’m really sort of perfect. Everyone else knows that. You’re just a little slow on the uptake.”<br><br>“Thank you for trusting me.”</blockquote>
</i><br>Jennifer L. Armentrout is one of authors who never disappoints. I’ve read most of her books, and I’ve loved them all. This is no exception. I love the feeling I get when I read her books. They are always the perfect combination of humor, sex, romance, wit, and fun. If you haven’t read <i>Wait for You</i>, I would say definitely read it before jumping into this one. At the end of this novella, you get a sneak peek for Jase and Teresa’s book, and I for one can’t wait!!! <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/2f4d3377-8ed6-44f2-a6da-336d340fe23b_zps6c62cc4f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382960282i/6301894.jpg" alt=" photo 2f4d3377-8ed6-44f2-a6da-336d340fe23b_zps6c62cc4f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="15080761161676965726" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer14326071886431415719"><br/>4.5 Stars<br/><br/><b>Loved This Companion POV</b><br/><br/>I just finished the first book of this duet "Wait For You" where we read Avery's POV. I immediately wanted to read Cam's POV, and so glad I did. His perspective of everything that was happening in their relationship was as fascinating and entertaining as I expected. I enjoyed it even more than the first book, as Cam is as delectable and enchanting as they come. <br/><br/>Cam could have his pick of any girl on campus, he is just that good looking and popular, but is intrigu</span>
  <span id="freeText14326071886431415719" style="display:none"><br />4.5 Stars<br /><br /><b>Loved This Companion POV</b><br /><br />I just finished the first book of this duet "Wait For You" where we read Avery's POV. I immediately wanted to read Cam's POV, and so glad I did. His perspective of everything that was happening in their relationship was as fascinating and entertaining as I expected. I enjoyed it even more than the first book, as Cam is as delectable and enchanting as they come. <br /><br />Cam could have his pick of any girl on campus, he is just that good looking and popular, but is intrigued and attracted to Avery. From the moment they plowed into each other on the way to class on college campus, she is the only girl he wants to hook up with. Over and over, he asks her to go out with him, and over and over she says "No!" She is unlike anyone he has ever met, a puzzle, a mystery, a red-headed knockout. He wants her in his life. He wants her bad! Avery on the other hand, seems to be immune to his obvious charm, or at least she is trying her best. Cam is determined to wear her down little by little.<br /><br />Avery went through pure hell as a teenager. Her parents, high school classmates and supposed friends hated her for something they assumed she did. She has been treated as the town pariah since age fourteen after attending a Halloween party, where things went from great to horribly wrong in a matter of moments. She yearns for normalcy in her life once again, and hopes to find it far, far from home on a college campus, where no one knows her name or anything about her past.<br /><br />Cam and Avery's relationship is a total slow burn, and I loved it!<br /><br />I encourage you to first read book one "Wait For You" to get the entire back story, before delving into this fast paced, could not put down, point of view from Cam, the sexy, engaging and hilarious H.</span>

<div id="review_611683029" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/611683029" />
    <a title="Patrycja" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6852653-patrycja"><img alt="Patrycja" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1586460589p2/6852653.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/611683029?book_show_action=true">May 10, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Patrycja" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Patrycja" href="/user/show/6852653-patrycja">Patrycja</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=arc-s">arc-s</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=2013">2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=must-read">must-read</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer611683029" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8933406595094673937"><br/><b> 4.5 stars </b><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381513202i/4964720._SX540_.jpg' width='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>How the describe the best, the feeling of utter love for a book as sweet and beautiful as Trust in Me? It’s hard to write something meaningful, when already everything I could say about Jennifer L Armentrout has been said. It’s possibly the hundreth time, I wrote that everything she writes touches me somehow. Sometimes, I get kick ass, fast paced and full of suspense novels that rock my world, and from time to time, I get beautiful, tear jerking, heart melting stories like Trust in Me</span>
  <span id="freeText8933406595094673937" style="display:none"><br><b> 4.5 stars </b><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381513202i/4964720._SX540_.jpg" width="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>How the describe the best, the feeling of utter love for a book as sweet and beautiful as Trust in Me? It’s hard to write something meaningful, when already everything I could say about Jennifer L Armentrout has been said. It’s possibly the hundreth time, I wrote that everything she writes touches me somehow. Sometimes, I get kick ass, fast paced and full of suspense novels that rock my world, and from time to time, I get beautiful, tear jerking, heart melting stories like Trust in Me. But I never leave disappointed. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381513202i/4964721._SY540_.jpg" width="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Cam’s point of view throws some light on unanswered questions from Avery’s part of story. Everything unfolds and unravels on our eyes as Jennifer L Armentrout effortlessly shows us the boy, we fell in love with. While reading Trust in Me, I’ve not only reread Wait for You, but in the most stunning way, I was showed a really well done psychological portrait of a young man in love. <br><br>It was amazing to see everything that went through Cameron’s head. Every thought, every emotion, was pictured in the best way possible - it was sincere, simple yet complicated and realistic. I swooned to many times to count over Cam’s cookies and his turtle. Now, I have a soft spot for these freaky little pets. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381513202i/4964722._SY540_.jpg" width="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Trust in Me was entincing and captivating, yet still strongly in Armentrout witty, sassy style, with great sense of humour as well as purely hot. I was able to see more crazy and funny scenes involving Ollie and Jase, and I can honestly say that next story in this series will knock my socks off. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381513202i/4964723.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For those of you who are worried Trust in Me would be boring, rewrite of Wait for You, you are mistaken. <br><br>Overall, I loved the ride through Cam’s wild and untamed mind. Armentrout made a good job to keep me entertained enough not to regret reading Trust in Me. On the contrary, she made this story more complex and I drooled over Cam and his cookies for over five hours ;)<br><br><i> *ARC provided by publisher, Willam Morrow via Edelweiss in exchange for honest review* </i><br><br><br><br><b><br>CHECK MY BLOG: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://smokinhotbookblog.blogspot.com/">http://smokinhotbookblog.blogspot.com/</a><br>LIKE ME ON FACEBOOK: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.facebook.com/smokinhotbookblog?ref=stream&amp;hc_location=stream">https://www.facebook.com/smokinhotboo...</a><br>FOLLOW ME ON TWITTER: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://twitter.com/BlogSmokin">https://twitter.com/BlogSmokin</a><br></b></span>

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer686235581" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9417576885047357436"><b> 4.5 COOKIES AND CAM STARS!!!</b><br/><br/><u>Note</u>: I feel like what I’m about to say is common knowledge, but I need to say it before I see <i>another</i> review rating it 2-3 stars because of this reason. This book is a <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17314430.Wait_for_You__Wait_for_You___1_' title='Wait for You (Wait for You, #1) by J. Lynn' rel='nofollow noopener'>Wait for You</a> novella in Cam’s POV so there is bound to be overlap. If you thought otherwise, PLEASE read the first sentence of the blurb. Don’t make yourself look like an idiot by stating in your review you thought this was book 2 about Cam and Avery.**End rant**<br/><br/><u>
  <b>My casting</b>
</u>:<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382119142i/5678332._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><u>
  <b>The turtle</b>
</u>:<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382120082ra/5679022.gif' width='350' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><u>In order </u></span>
  <span id="freeText9417576885047357436" style="display:none"><b> 4.5 COOKIES AND CAM STARS!!!</b><br><br><u>Note</u>: I feel like what I’m about to say is common knowledge, but I need to say it before I see <i>another</i> review rating it 2-3 stars because of this reason. This book is a <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17314430.Wait_for_You__Wait_for_You___1_" title="Wait for You (Wait for You, #1) by J. Lynn" rel="nofollow noopener">Wait for You</a> novella in Cam’s POV so there is bound to be overlap. If you thought otherwise, PLEASE read the first sentence of the blurb. Don’t make yourself look like an idiot by stating in your review you thought this was book 2 about Cam and Avery.**End rant**<br><br><u>
  <b>My casting</b>
</u>:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382119142i/5678332._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><u>
  <b>The turtle</b>
</u>:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382120082ra/5679022.gif" width="350" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><u>In order to <i>fully</i> enjoy this book</u>:<br><br>- <b>
  <i>Don't</i>
</b> re-read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17314430.Wait_for_You__Wait_for_You___1_" title="Wait for You (Wait for You, #1) by J. Lynn" rel="nofollow noopener">Wait for You</a>. You will find certain chapters repetitive. It's been almost half a year since I last read the first book so everything I read, I felt like I experienced again. I love that feeling!<br>- Make sure you're in the mood for something lighthearted. Yes, I know Avery went through a bad ordeal when she was young, but the overall tone I got was lighthearted. <br>- Have food nearby. I was starving. All those yummy cookies and goodies. My slice of heaven: cookies, cake, and Cam. Mmmmmmm...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382119481ra/5678503.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Prior to reading this book, I had hit an all new low in my book funk. I had books by authors I LOVED and I DNF’d the lot of them (I’ll go back sometime). I pinned my hopes on J. Lynn to bring back my reading mojo and yep. This woman did it. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382186047ra/5741231.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I’m not going to go into specific plot details since it was in book 1, but I want to emphasize that this is <b>
  <i>truly</i>
</b> Cam’s version of Wait for You. You get to see Cam’s thoughts about his past secrets, his innate kindness towards women in general, not just Avery, and how he suffered from a semester long of blue balls. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382186047ra/5741232.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>“God, I sounded like a vagina.”</i>
</b> - Cam<br><br><b>I’M TOTALLY KIDDING!!</b> But really, Cam was the ultimate sweetie and he’s one of the few heroes I’d choose over an alpha male!! Plus, I just loved reading about Ollie from his point of view. Best summarization of Ollie in 2 lines:<br><br><b>
  <i>“How he gets laid on a regular basis is beyond me.”<br><br>“It’s the greatest mystery in life.”</i>
</b> - Cam and Jase<br><br>I really cannot pick on anything that was wrong with the book. Sure, I was frustrated with Avery and the plot was moving a little slow, but these were both vital parts of what made this Avery and Cam’s journey. It’s just them. How it worked out. How it’s supposed to be. <br><br>One more thing. Don’t miss this book because it’s just a retelling of the first. It’s not. The <i>
  <b>feels</b>
</i> and emotions are different. You didn’t get to experience the full Cam effect in the first book. You will now. Cam will charm the panties right off you.<br><br><b>
  <i>“And just think about it. If ‘cookie’ is a code word, whatever it symbolizes, it’s been in your mouth.”</i>
</b> <br><br>I need me one of those cookies!!! So if you're thinking twice about reading this book, Cam has something to tell you!<br><br><i>
  <b>"You're going in the wrong direction, sweetheart."</b>
</i><br><br><i>Copy kindly provided by publisher in exchange for an honest review. Please keep in mind that these quotes are from an ARC and are subject to change in the final edition.</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="9417576885047357436" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer756221246" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1185049125060183260">This is book #1.5 in the "Wait for You" series. The first book in this series was called "Wait for You" and it was about Avery and Cam's fall into love with each other. I read the first book a few years back, and then got side tracked onto other reads. I came across book 1.5 on my Kindle and decided it was time to revisit this series! I am so glad that I did! <br/><br/>I actually thought "Trust in Me" was a novella, and probably a short story. It is pretty much the same story as book one; but it is in Cam</span>
  <span id="freeText1185049125060183260" style="display:none">This is book #1.5 in the "Wait for You" series. The first book in this series was called "Wait for You" and it was about Avery and Cam's fall into love with each other. I read the first book a few years back, and then got side tracked onto other reads. I came across book 1.5 on my Kindle and decided it was time to revisit this series! I am so glad that I did! <br /><br />I actually thought "Trust in Me" was a novella, and probably a short story. It is pretty much the same story as book one; but it is in Cam's POV. This ended up being perfect for me to start with, considering I needed a refresher on Avery and Cam's relationship. If you are starting this series, and decide to jump into this right after the first book, just be warned that it is the same story, just in Cam's POV. For me and my bad memory, I was very happy I decided to read this one. I was also happy that even though it is considered book 1.5, it is 350 pages!!!<br /><br />All in all, I happy that I refreshed my memory so I can move on to the next book which is about Cam's sister, and his best friend!!!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="1185049125060183260" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <span id="freeText10072925755192172657" style="display:none"><b>
  <u>My Thoughts:</u>
</b><br><br><br>❥ Loved getting Cam's POV even if he was a tad on the cocky side and there wasn't really anything new. <br><br>❥ I did miss Avery though...you definitely need to read the first book to enjoy this one. <br><br>❥ Loved "Shortcake" and how it finally came out.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382595763i/6046091.jpg" width="300" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>❥ Could not put it down...and it can easily be read in one day.<br><br>❥ Is it weird that I liked reading about Cam suffering? I always liked him but it was great reading more of him through Cam's eyes. <br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379795831i/610350.jpg" width="400" height="030" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <u>Favorite quotes:</u>
</b><br><br>✿ “I’m beginning to think ‘cookie’ is a code word for something else.”<br><br>✿ Every time you eat something, you sound like you’re about to have an orgasm.” She flushed as she said that. “Or whatever.” <br><br>“Well, now you know what I sound like when I come.”<br><br>✿ “I’m going to marry that girl one day,” I heard myself say. <br><br>Jase choked on his beer and bent over, dragging in deep breaths. <br><br>“Holy shit.” I grinned.<br><br>✿ “Smile!” Ollie snapped a picture. “It’s like my two kids are going to prom.”<br><br>✿ “Fuck, Avery. Don’t ever doubt that I want you."<br><br>✿ “You liked?” <br><br>I coughed out a laugh. “I loved.” <br><br>“I’m a quick learner.”</span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer610907543" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2796073394930931120">I more then loved every page of <i>Trust in Me</i>. I had a really hard time putting it down. And once again, I fell in love with Cam. Crazy in love. I truly enjoyed being in his head and getting to know him better. He was just as delicious as I imagined he would be. But I have to admit, I kinda missed Avery. What a shocker! While i found her a bit annoying and boring in <i>Wait for You</i>, this doesn´t make much sense without knowing her story. There is no doubt that this author is talanted and I can´t wait</span>
  <span id="freeText2796073394930931120" style="display:none">I more then loved every page of <i>Trust in Me</i>. I had a really hard time putting it down. And once again, I fell in love with Cam. Crazy in love. I truly enjoyed being in his head and getting to know him better. He was just as delicious as I imagined he would be. But I have to admit, I kinda missed Avery. What a shocker! While i found her a bit annoying and boring in <i>Wait for You</i>, this doesn´t make much sense without knowing her story. There is no doubt that this author is talanted and I can´t wait to read the next book in this series.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381513202i/4964720._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="285" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book, or "long novella" was one of the most anticipated for me this year. And it didn´t disappoint. It was so amazing being in Cam´s head. Can he be more perfect? Where has he been all my life? He bakes, he cooks, he has a turtoise as a pet (so hilarious!). But I think it was his soul I fell for. He was so patient with Avery, he loved her so much and on top of that, he´s gorgeous and charming. I loved how much he fought for her and his pain when he waited for her (sorry Cam...) Sigh...he really is ne of my top book boyfriends ever!<br><br>I HIGHLY recommend this. It was almost impossible to put down once you started it! But read <i>Wait for You</i> first!</span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1794380302" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer7456214808014121390"><b> 4 Persistent Love Stars </b><br/><br/><b> What's it about? </b> The same story as <i> "Wait For You" </i> but from the guy's point of view.<br/><br/><b> The best bits: </b> It's so great to re-visit a story I loved so much. To be honest , it's been a couple of years since I read the original, but many scenes were familiar and I really enjoyed the characters again. Particularly Cam.<br/><br/><b> The worst bits: </b> As enjoyable as it is, it's just a rehash of the same story. <br/><br/><b> Recommended for: </b> Those that have read the preceding <i> "Wait for Me" </i> only. <br/></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/695577557" />

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/695577557?book_show_action=true">Aug 15, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads">Jacqueline&#39;s Reads</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=4-star-books">4-star-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer695577557" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16010060103986669694"><a href='http://imgur.com/A840rCX' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386250907i/7321116._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I loved Wait for You, it was just a sweet and semi tragic love-story, so when I heard there would be Cam’s POV, well I was ALL OVER THAT.<br/><br/>The thing I love about Jennifer’s books is that she writes heavily on dialogue, which I am a MAJOR fan of, so when it translates into an alternative POV book, you don’t get that much difference, except for the parts where Avery and Cam do not interact.<br/><br/>What worked for me is the Hero, I loved Cam in book 1 and I was eager to see how he felt and what he was th</span>
  <span id="freeText16010060103986669694" style="display:none"><a href="http://imgur.com/A840rCX" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386250907i/7321116._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I loved Wait for You, it was just a sweet and semi tragic love-story, so when I heard there would be Cam’s POV, well I was ALL OVER THAT.<br><br>The thing I love about Jennifer’s books is that she writes heavily on dialogue, which I am a MAJOR fan of, so when it translates into an alternative POV book, you don’t get that much difference, except for the parts where Avery and Cam do not interact.<br><br>What worked for me is the Hero, I loved Cam in book 1 and I was eager to see how he felt and what he was thinking. I enjoyed getting into Cam’s mind and feeling his affections towards Avery. I also enjoyed the part where he went home and we saw his interactions with his family. I am also happy this is a 1.5 book and not a full book 2 book, to me that makes a difference. Trust in Me, feels like it’s a little extra special book just for the fans and not a way for the author to make extra dough. This I like. Thank you Jennifer.<br><br>If you loved Wait for You and Cam, well, Trust in Me is the perfect little extra something.<br><br><b>Series Order<br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17314430.Wait_for_You__Wait_for_You___1_" title="Wait for You (Wait for You, #1) by J. Lynn" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1363819713s/17314430.jpg" alt="Wait for You (Wait for You, #1) by J. Lynn" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1376561229s/17860217.jpg" alt="Trust in Me (Wait for You, #1.5) by J.   <b>Actual rating: 3.5/5 Sweetie-Cam Stars</b>

That's why I got bored in the beginning and shamelessly skimmed through the rest of the book.<br/><br/>The only scene I appreciated is the same as that in Wait for You, which is the part when Cam surprises Avery on the holiday and this time, Cam's POV is quite interesting.<br/><blockquote>
  <i>I pivoted around, about to apologize when I hadn't apologi</i></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText16296652412008881852" style="display:none"><u>
  <b>Actual rating: 3.5/5 Sweetie-Cam Stars</b>
</u><br /><br />Basically, it's the retelling of the story in <i>Wait for You</i> from Cameron Hamilton's POV so there's nothing special or new in this one. That's why I got bored in the beginning and shamelessly skimmed through the rest of the book.<br /><br />The only scene I appreciated is the same as that in Wait for You, which is the part when Cam surprises Avery on the holiday and this time, Cam's POV is quite interesting.<br /><blockquote>
  <i>I pivoted around, about to apologize when I hadn't apologized for any other time I'd busted up into her apartment, but she was in the kitchen, practically airborne. Coming at me the way Teresa had when she greeted me. The same way my sister had launched herself at Jase.<br />I caught her, wrapping my arms around her waist as I stumbled back, hitting the counter. Shock radiated through me, quickly followed by a wild warmth that lit up my veins.<br />My arms tightened around her as she pressed her cheek to my chest and held on just as strongly as I held her. I dropped my face to the top of her head, inhaling her scent and soaking her response in, holding her close to my heart. <br />Avery inhaled a shaky breath and said, <b>"I missed you."</b></i>
</blockquote><br /><br />Similarly, if you still can't get enough of Camery (or generally, Cam), then I strongly suggest you read this one!</span>

<div id="review_3268242224" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3268242224" />
    <a title="Bookadmirer " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/103293496-bookadmirer"><img alt="Bookadmirer " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1601720853p2/103293496.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3268242224?book_show_action=true">Apr 18, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Bookadmirer " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Bookadmirer " href="/user/show/103293496-bookadmirer">Bookadmirer </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/103293496-bookadmirer?shelf=broken-heroine">broken-heroine</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3268242224" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2471711751301779107">Cameron was just perfect. I was sold on the scene when he makes breakfast for Avery.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1587205630ra/29313225.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>You might think what's a big deal on it? I am from a very male chauvinist family, so when I see a man making an effort for his woman in a book, I immediately love it.<br/><br/>I felt really bad for Avery. She is such a sweet and innocent girl. The rapist should rot in jail. Her parents were horrible. I am glad she left them and moved far away from them. Cameron was so patient with her. I wished the big revelation happened </span>
  <span id="freeText2471711751301779107" style="display:none">Cameron was just perfect. I was sold on the scene when he makes breakfast for Avery.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1587205630ra/29313225.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>You might think what's a big deal on it? I am from a very male chauvinist family, so when I see a man making an effort for his woman in a book, I immediately love it.<br><br>I felt really bad for Avery. She is such a sweet and innocent girl. The rapist should rot in jail. Her parents were horrible. I am glad she left them and moved far away from them. Cameron was so patient with her. I wished the big revelation happened a bit earlier,. It just happened towards the end and I kind of got bored.</span>

<div id="review_610914079" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/610914079" />
    <a title="AJ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3143126-aj"><img alt="AJ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406382884p2/3143126.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/610914079?book_show_action=true">May 09, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="AJ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="AJ" href="/user/show/3143126-aj">AJ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=drama">drama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=romantic">romantic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer610914079" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12916951066568088381"><b>Cameron Hamilton *dreamy sigh*. </b> <br/><br/>Definitely one of my fave book boyfriends EVER! And while my experience with the retelling of much loved books from the male POV has been a bit hit and miss, I absolutely loved this one! I just finished a reread of <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17314430.Wait_for_You__Wait_for_You___1_' title='Wait for You (Wait for You, #1) by J. Lynn' rel='nofollow noopener'>Wait for You</a>, so Cam and Avery’s story was all very fresh in my head when I started this book (what can I say? I was in the Cam-zone, with no intention of getting out of it :P). And even though it’s essentially the same story, I was still madly flippin</span>
  <span id="freeText12916951066568088381" style="display:none"><b>Cameron Hamilton *dreamy sigh*. </b> <br /><br />Definitely one of my fave book boyfriends EVER! And while my experience with the retelling of much loved books from the male POV has been a bit hit and miss, I absolutely loved this one! I just finished a reread of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17314430.Wait_for_You__Wait_for_You___1_" title="Wait for You (Wait for You, #1) by J. Lynn" rel="nofollow noopener">Wait for You</a>, so Cam and Avery’s story was all very fresh in my head when I started this book (what can I say? I was in the Cam-zone, with no intention of getting out of it :P). And even though it’s essentially the same story, I was still madly flipping pages, unable to get enough. <br /><br />Cam and Avery’s transition from friends to lovers is absolutely beautiful. Both hiding secrets, and with Avery struggling to recover from events in her past, there is a lot standing between them, but Cam’s determination to win Avery over, combined with the sizzling chemistry and genuine friendship between them, can only lead to amazing things. And their journey to find their HEA made me laugh, cry and swoon all over again. <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“I want you, Cam.”<br />“You have me … You so fucking have me.”</i>
</blockquote><br />(yeah, that’s a line from the first book, but it’s repeated in this book and I had to include it because it’s pretty awesome).<br /><br />There is a fair bit of new stuff in this book. We get to see a bit more of Cam’s family, as well as spend some more time with Jase and Ollie, and God, I love these boys! Funny and crass, but also thoughtful and supportive of their best friend. <br /><br /><blockquote><i>“You’re spending a lot of time with this girl.” <br />“Whoa!” I stepped out of the shower, buck -ass naked, finding Ollie standing in the doorway of the bathroom. “What the hell, man?” <br />“What?” He shrugged. “Not like I haven’t seen your junk before.”<br /><br />“What is it about her?” he asked, sounding like he truly wanted to understand the attraction I could barely figure out. “She’s not like any other girl you’ve gone out with. She’s fucking awkward as hell and quiet. She’s pretty, but—” <br />“She’s fucking </i>beautiful<i>,” I cut in, daring him to disagree. <br />He didn’t. “Is she worth this?” <br />“Yes,” I said.</i></blockquote><br />There are some new scenes between Cam and Avery, which I thought was a great treat, and, of course, there are repeats of key scenes in <i>Wait for You</i>. But seeing Cam’s reaction to their banter, and getting his inner monologue along with it puts a completely different spin on things, and I loved every little interaction!<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“Cupping her cheek, I softly kissed her until her body relaxed under mine and then, shocking the hell out of me, her small hand ended up under my shirt, pressing against the bare skin of my abs. <br />It was like being branded. <br />Heat roared through my veins as my body jerked on reflex. Air punched from my lungs. She wanted to touch me? Holy hell, she could touch me. I pulled back, reached down and yanked my shirt over my head.”</i>
</blockquote><br />Yep, inside the head of a horny 22 year old male, is a very interesting place to be! And Cam’s thoughts are a sensational mix of thoughtful, sensitive, playful boyfriend…<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“I stood and went to her side. Taking her hands, I tugged her onto her feet and wrapped my arms around her waist. I lowered my head, brushing my lips across her cheek. “I’m serious about you, Avery. If you want me for real, you have me.” <br />Shortcake pressed her palms to my chest. “I want you for real.” <br />“Good to know.” I slanted my lips over hers. “Because, if not, this would get a whole lot awkward.”</i>
</blockquote><br />… and sex-crazed (though it must be said - respectful) College boy…<br /><br /><blockquote>“<i>I’d been taking things slow, so slow I wondered if I could go any slower. Every night I ended up going one on one with myself to the point that my hand was starting to get numb while I took notes in class.</i>”</blockquote><br />Getting to know him better just made me fall even harder for him. He is such a great guy, and remains at the top of my list of most amazing book boyfriends ever!<br /><br /><b>
  <blockquote>
    <i>“The truth was, if I was perfect, it was only because of her. It would only ever be because of her.”</i>
  </blockquote>
</b><br />I wouldn’t recommend reading this without having read <i>Wait for You</i> first, because it’s not a direct repeat, and you’ll need to know the full story before diving in, but this is a fabulous addition to the series - getting us close and personal with the incredible Cam, and giving us a bit of an intro to Jase and Theresa’s story coming up next and which I am SO looking forward to.<br /><br />I loved it – 4 stars.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="12916951066568088381" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1416978895" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1416978895" />
    <a title="⊱ Poppy ⊰" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/47555322-poppy"><img alt="⊱ Poppy ⊰" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1475924055p2/47555322.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1416978895?book_show_action=true">Oct 15, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="⊱ Poppy ⊰" class="user" itemprop="url" name="⊱ Poppy ⊰" href="/user/show/47555322-poppy">⊱ Poppy ⊰</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/47555322-poppy?shelf=multiple-pov">multiple-pov</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1416978895" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15241503464532653906">In Trust in Me (Wait For You #1.5) by J. Lynn, College student Cameron “Cam” Hamilton almost gets knocked off his feet when he meets Avery Morgansten for the first time. The pint-sized young woman with fiery red hair and gorgeous chocolate eyes captures his attention right away. Avery’s the only girl to turn him down for a date on campus. And she turns him down repeatedly to the point that it becomes an ongoing joke between them as they become close friends.<br/><br/><blockquote>‘Avery was such a mystery to me; a par</blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText15241503464532653906" style="display:none">In Trust in Me (Wait For You #1.5) by J. Lynn, College student Cameron “Cam” Hamilton almost gets knocked off his feet when he meets Avery Morgansten for the first time. The pint-sized young woman with fiery red hair and gorgeous chocolate eyes captures his attention right away. Avery’s the only girl to turn him down for a date on campus. And she turns him down repeatedly to the point that it becomes an ongoing joke between them as they become close friends.<br /><br /><blockquote>‘Avery was such a mystery to me; a paradox of innocence and allure–a mystery I was determined to solve.’</blockquote><br /><br />But Cam wants to take things to the next level with Avery. However, he gets a weird vibe that she’s hiding something from him and he wonders if someone may have hurt her in the past. He takes things slow with Avery, trying to gain her trust and help her build confidence. He hopes if he confesses about his own previous troubles, that she’ll reciprocate and clue him in on what’s now troubling her. All Cam knows is that he’s determined he can be the man Avery needs and that they can build a life together. Even if he has to woo her with homemade cookies, one batch at a time, to get her to agree.<br /><br /><blockquote>‘Turning my cheek, I pressed a kiss to the inside of her palm. “Thank you for trusting in me.”</blockquote><br />Trust in Me is the flip side to J Lynn’s incredible book Wait for You. This is Cam’s side of the story, and let me tell you, it doesn’t lose any of the intensity, humor or passion that we saw in book one. I know some readers aren’t that into reading two books about the same plot. But to me, it was definitely worth reading both Avery and Cam’s pov. I loved the storyline and felt that this gave us an insight into their feelings and why they dealt with things as they did.<br /><br /><blockquote>‘The initial zap, the shock of our lips together hadn’t faded. Dumbly I realized that love made it that way, making sure that a simple kiss never dulled, never lost its luster.’</blockquote><br /><br />I fell in love with Cam all over again when I read Trust in Me. How could you not? He is a sweet, sexy, charming, fun guy and he was perfect for Avery. I loved that Cam had a secret nickname for her (Shortcake) and that he was always trying to do what was right for her in any given situation. He has some anger issues like any young man, but he has learned the right and wrong way to deal with his emotions, which certainly gets tested throughout the story. Plus…how sweet is it that he baked her cookies and lots of chocolatey treats? What girl wouldn’t swoon over a guy who did that?<br /><br /><blockquote>“If you change your mind, I’ll be up for a while.”<br />“I’m not going to. Good night, Cam.”<br />Ouch. Damn. Shortcake just dismissed my ass. For some reason, that made me smile.</blockquote><br /><br />Cam and Avery have both been through very serious situations in the past and in some ways I think that may have helped them bond and to recognize certain emotional issues in each other. Those situations are definitely dark and not lighthearted, but J Lynn manages to keep the overall tone of the story fairly upbeat with some extremely smart and humorous dialogue.<br /><br />J Lynn’s Wait for You series is New Adult storytelling done exactly right. Whether you’re already a fan of the genre, or if you want a good place to start, you can’t go wrong with Wait for You and Trust in Me.<br /><br /><b>Cameron:</b><br />Cameron Hamilton is used to getting what he wants, especially when it comes to women. But when Avery Morgansten comes crashing into his life – literally – he finally meets the one person who can resist his soulful baby blues. But Cam’s not ready to give up. He can’t get the feisty and intriguing girl out of his head.<br /><br />Avery has secrets, secrets that keep her from admitting the feelings Cam knows she has for him. Will persistence (and some delicious homemade cookies) help him break down her barriers and gain her trust? Or will he be shut out of Avery’s life, losing his first real shot at the kind of love that lasts forever?</span>
  <a data-text-id="15241503464532653906" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_666011897" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/666011897" />
    <a title="Michelle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13126896-michelle"><img alt="Michelle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1505605297p2/13126896.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/666011897?book_show_action=true">Jul 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Michelle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Michelle" href="/user/show/13126896-michelle">Michelle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13126896-michelle?shelf=01-signed">01-signed</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer666011897" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14429713720506232486">I really wanted to give this a full 5 stars, but settled on 4 since we not too much was given in the way of new information to Cam & Avery's story. But I did just adore this. <br/><br/>I am not going to retell the story, that can be found here: <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/547946888' rel='nofollow noopener'>Review of Wait For You.</a><br/><br/>With the anticipation of this release I was starting to crave myself a little bit of Cam. So getting this was just that perfect fix I needed. Cam came across as such a sweetheart through Avery's eyes and I was so glad to see that when it's th</span>
  <span id="freeText14429713720506232486" style="display:none">I really wanted to give this a full 5 stars, but settled on 4 since we not too much was given in the way of new information to Cam &amp; Avery's story. But I did just adore this. <br><br>I am not going to retell the story, that can be found here: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/547946888" rel="nofollow noopener">Review of Wait For You.</a><br><br>With the anticipation of this release I was starting to crave myself a little bit of Cam. So getting this was just that perfect fix I needed. Cam came across as such a sweetheart through Avery's eyes and I was so glad to see that when it's their love story from his point of view, that it did not change - not one bit. Oh Cam...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/643520.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Cam has to be one of my favorite male characters that fall into the sweet category. He isn't your broken, possessive, alpha-male, kinky type hero. He is just a boy that when he loves, he loves you with all his heart and he loves you hard. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382680232ra/6119285.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And although we all know where they end up and how they got there, seeing the struggle from his side opened my eyes to something that I didn't feel when reading Wait For You. Avery was a bit annoying in her resistance to giving in to Cam and not seeing just how much he had fallen in love with her. But being able to see Cam want her to trust him and be honest with him and how hard it was for him during those times made my heart hurt for him. <br><br>And although this was pretty much just the same story as we have already read, it opens the door perfectly for the next book, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17558817.Be_with_Me__Wait_for_You___2_" title="Be with Me (Wait for You, #2) by J. Lynn" rel="nofollow noopener">Be with Me</a>. Jase and Cam's sister Teresa have what looks like quite a story to tell. The pairing of these two would make no sense without reading this book. And I have a feeling that as much as Cam made us weak in the knees, Jase's story is going to bring you to them. <br><br>If you're like me and read the first book back when it was released in early 2013 this not feel repetitive for you. If you recently read it, and it's still fresh in your mind, you might want to give yourself some time before reading. I realized that although I still recalled their story, there were little scenes here and there that I had forgotten and got to experience all over again. <br><br>I loved J. Lynn's writing style and could not find one fault with the perfectness that was Cam. </span>
  <a data-text-id="14429713720506232486" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_853991618" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/853991618" />
    <a title="Jeanne " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16160718-jeanne"><img alt="Jeanne " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1410740995p2/16160718.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/853991618?book_show_action=true">Feb 13, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jeanne " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jeanne " href="/user/show/16160718-jeanne">Jeanne </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer853991618" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2153698572434275682"> <b>4.5 stars!!!</b> <br/><br/><b> " I'm beginning to think 'cookie' is code word for something else"</b> <br/><br/>Swooon, I think anyone would love to be Cameron Hamilton's Shortcake after reading this!!<br/><br/><a href='http://imgur.com/cVguozn' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392593729ra/8581903.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/> I liked this story much more in Cameron's POV which seems funny, but this was one of the most entertaining male POV books I've ever read. I kind of forgot a lot of details from Wait for You, so I didn't really mind that this was for the most part just retelling that story. I've seen this described as a novella, but that is</span>
  <span id="freeText2153698572434275682" style="display:none"> <b>4.5 stars!!!</b> <br><br><b> " I'm beginning to think 'cookie' is code word for something else"</b> <br><br>Swooon, I think anyone would love to be Cameron Hamilton's Shortcake after reading this!!<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/cVguozn" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392593729ra/8581903.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br> I liked this story much more in Cameron's POV which seems funny, but this was one of the most entertaining male POV books I've ever read. I kind of forgot a lot of details from Wait for You, so I didn't really mind that this was for the most part just retelling that story. I've seen this described as a novella, but that isn't the case, it's 352 pages. Cameron is all kinds of adorable. He is sweet, loving, protective and hilarious. I love his cocky humor and basically had a cheesy grin on my face half the time I was reading this. If someone is just starting this series, I would recommend reading this instead of Wait For You if you are only planning to read one of them. Another thing I liked about this book is you get a little peek into Jace and Cam's family which is really fun before reading book #2 Be with Me:) I loved it! This is my favorite out of the three so far, all because of Cam.</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ge7GhIKgBpe4kpBB20UmDSVSY3u5xyMHdDYTogaWbuKv2cyuwaDiZQaTuj0XkwjEMAbTaWpE03sH+Q05gBUJQg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('adHbx4XX+ARGkHo8sGLVx+nrenlod8su4H++0JmnxMdH5tHtxtcc9viRUEB8tPsO/L/Ka7v0O1KTsKBLHySjZw==')})
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer12238698299789452691">Hey Guys! Please note: I don't send out ARCs for review. If you're interested in reviewing a book of mine before release date, please contact the appropriate publisher. I also do NOT check my Goodreads email.<br/><br/>To email me, please use the below addy. <br/>jenniferlarmentrout@live.com<br/><br/># 1 New York Times and # 1 International Bestselling author Jennifer lives in Charles Town, West Virginia. All the rumors yo</span>
  <span id="freeText12238698299789452691" style="display:none">Hey Guys! Please note: I don't send out ARCs for review. If you're interested in reviewing a book of mine before release date, please contact the appropriate publisher. I also do NOT check my Goodreads email.<br /><br />To email me, please use the below addy. <br />jenniferlarmentrout@live.com<br /><br /># 1 New York Times and # 1 International Bestselling author Jennifer lives in Charles Town, West Virginia. All the rumors you’ve heard about her state aren’t true. When she’s not hard at work writing. she spends her time reading, watching really bad zombie movies, pretending to write, hanging out with her husband and her Jack Russell Loki. In early 2015, Jennifer was diagnosed with retinitis pigmentosa, a group of rare genetic disorders that involve a breakdown and death of cells in the retina, eventually resulting in loss of vision, among other complications. Due to this diagnosis, educating people on the varying degrees of blindness has become of passion of hers, right alongside writing, which she plans to do as long as she can. <br /><br />Her dreams of becoming an author started in algebra class, where she spent most of her time writing short stories….which explains her dismal grades in math. Jennifer writes young adult paranormal, science fiction, fantasy, and contemporary romance. She is published with Tor, HarperCollins Avon and William Morrow, Entangled Teen and Brazen, Disney/Hyperion and Harlequin Teen. Her Wicked Series has been optioned by PassionFlix. Jennifer has won numerous awards, including the 2013 Reviewers Choice Award for Wait for You, the 2015 Editor’s Pick for Fall With Me, and the 2014/2015 Moerser-Jugendbuch- Jury award for Obsidian. Her young adult romantic suspense novel DON’T LOOK BACK was a 2014 nominated Best in Young Adult Fiction by YALSA. Her adult romantic suspense novel TILL DEATH was a Amazon Editor’s Pick and iBook Book of the Month. Her young adult contemporary THE PROBLEM WITH FOREVER is a 2017 RITA Award Winner in Young Adult Fiction. She also writes Adult and New Adult contemporary and paranormal romance under the name J. Lynn. She is published by Entangled Brazen and HarperCollins.<br /><br />She is the owner of ApollyCon and The Origin Event, the successful annual events that features over hundred bestselling authors in Young Adult, New Adult, and Adult Fiction, panels, parties, and more.</span>
